NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
Matsushita Air-conditioning India Private Limited
It is hereby notified to the general public that the company has passed a special resolution to wind up the company by
Members Voluntary Winding-up under Section 484 of the companies Act, 1956 and Mr. S. Srikanth, Chartered Accountant, having
office at ‘SREE SAI NIVAS’ No. 4 Balaji Avenue, 1st Street, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017, is appointed as Liquidator of the Company
for the purpose of winding up of the company.

29th July 2011.
